Careers Homepage\",\"engFallback\",\"No matching Engineering or Data role? {{engFallbackCTA}} and we'll be in touch if a role comes up which matches your skillset.\",\"engFallbackCTA\",\"Leave us your contact information\",\"howWeHire\",{\"_3991\":3992,\"_3993\":3994},\"title\",\"How we hire\",\"content\",\"\u003cp\u003eWe hire people, not resumes. Our hiring process is designed to learn more about you, your mindset, and the impact you can have at Shopify.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eBelow you will learn more about our hiring process. The order and number of interviews may vary depending on the role and team you are applying for.\u003c/p\u003e\",\"questions\",{\"_3997\":3998,\"_4003\":4004,\"_4007\":4008},\"process\",{\"_3999\":4000,\"_4001\":4002},\"question\",\"The process\",\"answer\",\"\u003ch4\u003e1. Apply\u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e Select 1–2 roles that you believe are the best fit for yourself and your career. Don’t forget to check the requirements before you submit, as each role may have different ones. \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e2. Initial call\u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e Depending on the role, we may set up a 15–30 minute phone or virtual conversation with a recruiter or hiring manager, where you can ask questions and tell us what you’re interested in. Get the intel on who you’ll meet and technical exercises. We’ll also use this information to help explore other roles that may be a better fit. For R\u0026amp;D applicants, you'll pass this step and go directly into pair programming before heading to The Life Story; a member of the Talent Acquisition team will share all the details! \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e3. Craft Assessment\u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003eA 60-75 minute interview. As part of your interview process, you will be interviewed by at least one person within your craft to dive into what you are best at. This is an opportunity for us to learn how you approach your craft and for you and your interviewer to nerd out together.\u003c/p\u003e \u003cp\u003eAs part of this step, you'll also take a brief predictive assessment to help us learn more about how you approach problems, think critically, and notice the details.\u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e \u003ch4\u003e4. The Life Story\u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003eA 30-60 minute conversation-style interview with a recruiter. The Life Story interview is about understanding the themes of your career journey so far, what you have learnt, and how you made a difference. We’re interested in the trophies and the bruises: the problems you solved, the challenges you encountered, the decisions you made, and the lessons you learned. The best way to prepare for the Life Story interview is to spend time reflecting on all the experiences that brought you to where you are today: the hits and misses, the pivotal points, your proudest moments, and the hardest projects. Then, be ready to settle into a genuine, two-sided conversation.\u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e 5. Meet the team\u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e You’ll meet with 3–5 future co-workers for up to an hour each. Depending on the role, we may ask how you’d solve a problem and communicate it to the team. \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e6. Decision\u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e Your hiring team will take the time to meet before getting back to you. This will be made based on feedback from Shopify team members of varying levels of seniority, experiences, and perspectives. \u003c/p\u003e\",\"hiring\",{\"_3999\":4005,\"_4001\":4006},\"Hiring FAQ\",\"\u003ch4\u003e Can I apply for more than one job? \u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e Yes. Please limit to 2 applications within a 30-day period. During the process, your recruiter will also help you explore the best options for you. \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e Who can I turn to if I have questions throughout the interview process? \u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e Our recruiters and coordinators will be supporting you throughout the process. Feel free to ask them questions about what to expect, who you will meet, and more. \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e How long is the hiring process typically? \u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e Timelines will vary depending on the role and number of applicants. \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e What should I wear to my interview? \u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e Come as you are. Maybe you think best in a three-piece suit; maybe you have a favorite t-shirt and jeans combo—we're happy as long as you’re comfortable. \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e I have applied/interviewed in the past and wasn’t selected. Can I apply again? \u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e Absolutely. If re-applying for the same role, we encourage you to first gain additional experience. For engineering roles, we ask that you wait 6–12 months before applying again. \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e When can I expect to hear back after I have applied? \u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e Due to the large volume of applications we get every day, we can only follow up with candidates we would like to move forward with in the interview process. \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e What if I need an accommodation for the interview? \u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e No problem. If you're selected for an interview and need any accommodations, please let your recruiter know. \u003c/p\u003e \u003ch4\u003e How does onboarding work? \u003c/h4\u003e \u003cp\u003e We've revamped our onboarding process so information gathering, team communication, and workflows happen as smoothly as possible. \u003c/p\u003e\",\"pay\",{\"_3999\":4009,\"_4001\":4010},\"How We Pay\",\"\u003cp\u003e Everything of value that you receive and experience at Shopify makes up your total rewards. That includes benefits, perks, and learning and growth opportunities. It also includes a world-class compensation system that's first-of-its-kind. \u003c/p\u003e \u003cp\u003e Under the old industry structure, there was no one place to go to understand exactly how much you earned. You’d find base salary on your pay stub and your equity in another, made even more complicated by vesting schedules, stock-market unpredictability and bonuses tied to company performance. Trying to figure out how much you’d actually take home in a year was a pain. Our Flex Comp system lays everything out simply in a one-stop shop. \u003c/p\u003e \u003cp\u003eThe Shopify Flex Comp system allows you to:\u003c/p\u003e \u003cp\u003e\u003cul\u003e \u003cli\u003e Choose your own balance of total reward between cash (base salary) and equity (RSUs and options). \u003c/li\u003e \u003cli\u003e Change your balance throughout the year as your priorities do. (Maybe you’re buying a house, or planning for long-term investment, or want a change for no reason at all — we don’t need to know!) \u003c/li\u003e \u003cli\u003e Increase your compensation as your positive impact on Shopify’s mission grows. \u003c/li\u003e \u003c/ul\u003e\u003c/p\u003e \u003cp\u003e Shopify has always been a company of curious, talented, and innovative people who believe in making meaningful change in the world. We also believe in making sure you’re rewarded for your contribution to making commerce better for everyone. \u003c/p\u003e\",\"aboutShopify\",{\"_3991\":511,\"_3993\":4013},\"\u003cp\u003eOpportunity is not evenly distributed. Shopify puts independence within reach for anyone with a dream to start a business. We propel entrepreneurs and enterprises to scale the heights of their potential. Since 2006, we’ve grown to over 8,300 employees and generated over $1 trillion in sales for millions of merchants in 175 countries. \u003c/p\u003e \u003cp\u003e This is life-defining work that directly impacts people’s lives as much as it transforms your own. This is putting the power of the few in the hands of the many, is a future with more voices rather than fewer, and is creating more choices instead of an elite option.\u003c/p\u003e\",\"aboutYou\",{\"_3991\":4016,\"_3993\":4017,\"_4018\":4019,\"_4020\":4021,\"_4030\":4031},\"About you\",\"\u003cp\u003eMoving at our pace brings a lot of change, complexity, and ambiguity—and a little bit of chaos. Shopifolk thrive on that and are comfortable being uncomfortable. That means Shopify is not the right place for everyone.\u003c/p\u003e\",\"beforeApply\",\"Before you apply, consider if you can:\",\"considerAction\",[4022,4023,4024,4025,4026,4027,4028,4029],\"Care deeply about what you do and about making commerce better for everyone\",\"Excel by seeking professional and personal hypergrowth\",\"Keep up with an unrelenting pace (the week, not the quarter)\",\"Be resilient and resourceful in face of ambiguity and thrive on (rather than endure) change\",\"Bring critical thought and opinion\",\"Put AI agents and tools to work on the tasks they're built for, and focus on the work only humans can do\",\"Embrace differences and disagreement to get shit done and move forward\",\"Work digital-first for your daily work\",\"disclaimer\",\"We may use AI-enabled tools to screen, select, and assess applications. We hire interns and place them on teams we think they’d be successful on. We place interns on teams based on their experience, interest, and what works best for Shopify. We hire interns exclusively into Data and Engineering internships.\\n\\nData Internships:\\n\\nWe’re looking for interns to work in the following areas:\\n\\n - Data Engineering to architect and manage the expansive data pipelines that fuel everything from product analytics to merchant-facing data products.\\n\\n - Product Data Science to deeply understand our products, tell their stories and figure out how to make them 10x better.\\n\\nEngineering Internships:\\n\\nWe are looking primarily for interns to fill a large number of internship roles in Software Engineering:\\n\\n - Software Engineering: to craft the code that powers commerce, creating the extendable products that scale the entire commerce stack.\\n\\nCandidates with previous experience in the following areas may be considered for internships within these areas:\\n\\n - Applied Machine Learning Engineering: to use extensive data to build products and create and fine-tune ML models.\\n\\n - Infrastructure Engineering: to build and develop the blocks that move all of Shopify forward.\\n\\n - Security Engineering: to detect, evaluate, and address security threats to Shopify and its merchants.\\n\\nShopify is a big part of the Ruby and Rails communities, and we’re constantly improving our codebase to make it even better. You do not need prior Rails experience to apply to this internship!\\n\\nWorking at Shopify:\\n\\n - You must be legally entitled to work in the location they are applying to for the entire duration of the Fall 2026 internship (September 8th to December 18th, 2026). Shopify does not provide immigration support to intern candidates.\\n\\n - This internship is a 4 month long, full-time, paid experience - interns are expected not to be enrolled in school full-time while working at Shopify.\\n\\nAs an Intern you must be able to work from one of our offices:\\n\\nCanada\\n\\n - Montréal, Québec (490 Rue De la Gauchetière O)\\n\\n - Ottawa, Ontario (151 O’Connor Street)\\n\\n - Toronto, Ontario (620 King West)\\n\\nUSA\\n\\n - Bellevue (1100 112th Ave NE, Bellevue, WA 98004)\\n\\n - New York (85 10th Ave, New York City, New York 10011)\\n\\nPlease note: if you don’t currently live in one of the above cities, you must be willing and able to relocate for in-office experiences at one of these offices. If successful in your application, we will match you to a team when you start at Shopify. We’re unable to accommodate requests for particular teams and location changes once an offer is signed.\\n\\nOnboarding:\\n\\n - Interns must be located in their office city by the first day of onboarding (September 8, 2026) ready to work 9:00am - 5:00pm. Interns cannot work from outside of the country they are hired in during their internship.\\n\\nQualifications:\\n\\n - You love challenging yourself with projects or hacking just for fun\\n\\n - You are a constant learner\\n\\n - You have a passion for solving tough problems with code\\n\\n - You take ownership of the projects you work on\\n\\n - You enjoy research and figuring out how pieces of an entire project work\\n\\n - You take pride in creating simple solutions to complex problems\\n\\n - You have a strong commitment to quality\\n\\nAdditional Information\\n\\nIn your application:\\n\\n 1. Include your resume\\n\\n 2. Answer all of the application questions\\n\\n 3. Once you submit your application, and if you move forward in our process, you’ll then be emailed a series of mandatory assessments to complete. These will help assess your technical skills and your likelihood of success at Shopify.\\n\\nWe know that applying for internships can be time-consuming, and we truly appreciate your effort. The Early Talent Programs Team are actual real live people (👋🏻) and we’re looking forward to learning more about you through your application.\\n\\nApplications will close May 7th at 11:59pm (ET).\\n\\n-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n\\n\\nDESCRIPTION DU POSTE\\n\\nConsultez notre FAQ (questions fréquentes) sur les stages en ingénierie et en données https://internships.shopify.com/a/faq/ pour répondre à toutes vos questions sur le programme de stages chez Shopify.\\n\\nÊtre stagiaire chez Shopify :\\n\\nNotre processus de recrutement est unique. Nous recrutons des stagiaires et les plaçons dans des équipes où nous pensons qu’ils auront du succès. Nous attribuons les stagiaires aux équipes en fonction de leur expérience, de leurs intérêts et de ce qui convient le mieux à Shopify. Nous recrutons des stagiaires exclusivement pour des stages en données et en ingénierie.\\n\\nStages en données :\\n\\nNous recherchons des stagiaires pour travailler dans les domaines suivants:\\n\\n - Ingénierie des données pour concevoir et gérer les pipelines de données étendus qui alimentent tout, des analyses de produits aux produits de données destinés aux marchands.\\n\\n - Science des données produit pour comprendre en profondeur nos produits, raconter leur histoire et trouver comment les améliorer de façon décuplée.\\n\\nStages en ingénierie:\\n\\nNous cherchons principalement des stagiaires pour pourvoir un grand nombre de postes de stage en génie logiciel :\\n\\n - Ingénierie logiciel: pour concevoir le code qui propulse le commerce, en créant des produits extensibles qui font évoluer l'ensemble de la pile commerciale.\\n\\nLes candidats ayant une expérience préalable dans les domaines suivants pourraient être considérés pour des stages dans ces domaines:\\n\\n - Ingénierie en apprentissage automatique appliqué: pour utiliser des données exhaustives afin de développer des produits et de créer et affiner des modèles d'apprentissage automatique.\\n\\n - Ingénierie d'infrastructure: pour construire et développer les composantes qui font avancer l'ensemble de Shopify.\\n\\n - Ingénierie de la sécurité: pour détecter, évaluer et traiter les menaces de sécurité auxquelles Shopify et ses marchands font face.\\n\\nShopify joue un rôle important au sein des communautés Ruby et Rails, et nous améliorons constamment notre base de code pour la rendre encore meilleure. Pas besoin d’avoir déjà travaillé avec Rails pour postuler à ce stage!\\n\\nTravailler chez Shopify :\\n\\n - Vous devez être légalement autorisé à travailler au Canada pendant toute la durée du stage d'automne 2026 (du 8 septembre au 18 décembre 2026). Shopify ne propose pas de soutien en matière d’immigration pour les stagiaires.\\n\\n - Ce stage est une expérience rémunérée à temps plein d’une durée de quatre mois. Les stagiaires doivent être disponibles à temps plein et ne pas être inscrits à des études à temps plein pendant leur stage chez Shopify.\\n\\nEn tant que stagiaire, vous devez être en mesure de travailler depuis l'un de nos bureaux:\\n\\nCanada\\n\\n - Montréal, Québec (490 Rue De la Gauchetière O)\\n\\n - Ottawa, Ontario (151, rue O'Connor)\\n\\n - Toronto, Ontario (620 King Ouest)\\n\\nÉtats-Unis\\n\\n - Bellevue (1100 112th Ave NE, Bellevue, WA 98004)\\n\\n - New York (85 10th Ave, New York City, New York 10011)\\n\\nVeuillez noter : si vous ne résidez pas actuellement dans l'une des villes mentionnées ci-dessus, vous devez être disposé et en mesure de vous relocaliser pour des expériences en présentiel dans l'un de ces bureaux. Si votre candidature est retenue, nous vous assignerons à une équipe au moment de votre arrivée chez Shopify. Nous ne sommes pas en mesure d’accepter les demandes de placement dans une équipe précise ni les changements de lieu une fois l’offre signée.\\n\\nIntégration :\\n\\n - Les stagiaires doivent être présents dans leur ville de travail dès le premier jour de leur intégration (le 8 septembre 2026) et être prêts à travailler de 9 h à 17 h. Vous ne pouvez pas travailler en dehors du pays prévu durant votre stage.\\n\\nProfil recherché :\\n\\n - Vous souhaitez vous lancer des défis, que ce soit à travers des projets ou du hacking pour le plaisir.\\n\\n - Vous avez toujours soif d’apprendre.\\n\\n - Vous aimez résoudre des problèmes complexes avec du code.\\n\\n - Vous travaillez de manière autonome et prenez pleinement en charge les projets qui vous sont confiés.\\n\\n - Vous aimez la recherche et comprendre comment les différentes parties d’un projet s’articulent.\\n\\n - Vous savez trouver des solutions simples aux problèmes complexes.\\n\\n - La qualité est au cœur de votre travail.\\n\\nInformations supplémentaires\\n\\nDans votre candidature :\\n\\n 1. Ajoutez votre CV\\n\\n 2. Répondez à toutes les questions indiquées\\n\\n 3. Une fois votre candidature soumise, si vous êtes retenu pour la suite du processus, nous vous enverrons par e-mail une liste d’évaluations obligatoires à compléter. Celles-ci permettront d’évaluer vos compétences techniques et vos chances de succès chez Shopify.\\n\\nNous savons que la recherche d’un stage peut être longue et pénible, et nous vous remercions sincèrement pour votre investissement. Notre équipe du programme de stages est composée de vraies personnes (👋🏻) et nous avons hâte d’en apprendre davantage sur vous à travers votre candidature.\\n\\nLes candidatures doivent être soumises avant le 7 mai à 23h59 (heure de l'Est).\\n\\n\\n\",\"descriptionHtml\",\"\u003cp\u003eRead through our\u003ca target=\\\"_blank\\\" rel=\\\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\\\" href=\\\"https://internships.shopify.com/a/faq/\\\"\u003e\u003cu\u003e Internships FAQ\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e to help answer any questions you may have about internships at Shopify.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBeing a Shopify Intern:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eOur hiring process is unique.
